Watson Standard has migrated to an updated ERP Computer system which is used to determine chemical usage.  During the migration to this system, the composition of all raw materials used at all Watson Standard facilities were redefined using updated information received from our raw material suppliers.  There was also an improvement to the scheme used to define composition of raw materials to the chemical (CAS#) level.  This resulted in improved ability to aggregate small usages of chemicals spread out among many raw materials used in production, and hence, additional chemicals identified and reported for 2013 as being used above their reportable thresholds. 15225WTSNSCORNE	1313211655535	000050000	FORMALDEHYDE	TRI	2013	WATSON STANDARD CO (NEVILLE ISLAND PLANT)	2895 GRAND AVE	PITTSBURGH	ALLEGHENY	PA	15225			YES	NO	NO	NO								325510						40.5041	-80.10197	883495889								WATSON INDUSTRIES INC	834950552	There is an increase in the number of chemicals reported over reporting year 2012.  Watson Standard has migrated to an updated ERP Computer system which is used to determine chemical usage.  During the migration to this system, the composition of all raw materials used at all Watson Standard facilities were redefined using updated information received from our raw material suppliers.  There was also an improvement to the scheme used to define composition of raw materials to the chemical (CAS#) level.  This resulted in improved ability to aggregate small usages of chemicals spread out among many raw materials used in production, and hence, additional chemicals identified and reported for 2013 as being used above their reportable thresholds. Although we continue to implement various procedures to reduce waste, we have purchased another business that we are in the process of moving to this location.  Therefore, our waste is expected to increase substantially over the next 2 years due to increased production.  We are and will continue to evaluate options for source reduction.
